<li>to permeate</li>
<li>to infiltrate</li>
<li>to perforate</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проникать.html>проника́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pronikátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проникаться.html>проника́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pronikátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проникнуться.html>прони́кнуться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be imbued <i>(with)</i>, to imbue one's mind <i>(with)</i>, to be filled <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проникаться.html>проника́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сознание.html>созна́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>до́лга</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pronikátʹsja</b> soznánijem dólga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be imbued/filled with a sense of duty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проникаться.html>проника́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pronikátʹsja</b> ljubóvʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be inspired with love</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проникать.html>проника́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pronikátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">проникнове́н(ие)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proniknovén(ije)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проникнуть.html>прони́кнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proníknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проникать.html>проника́ть</a></b>) (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative)
</p>
<ol><li>to penetrate</li>
<li>to permeate</li>
<li>to infiltrate</li>
<li>to perforate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проникновение.html>проникнове́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">proniknovénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проникновенный.html>проникнове́нный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">proniknovénnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́к</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нуть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3°a[(6)].      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:проникать.html>проника́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>про-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-ник-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проникнуться.html>прони́кнуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proníknutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проникаться.html>проника́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be imbued <i>(with)</i>, to imbue one's mind <i>(with)</i>, to be filled <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проникнуться.html>прони́кнуться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сознание.html>созна́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>до́лга</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proníknutʹsja</b> soznánijem dólga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be imbued/filled with a sense of duty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проникнуться.html>прони́кнуться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proníknutʹsja</b> ljubóvʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be inspired with love</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проникнуться.html>прони́кнуться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proníknutʹsja</b> drug k drúgu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to feel an affection for one another</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проникнуть.html>прони́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proníknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́к</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нуть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проницательный.html>проница́тельный</a> (10788)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">проница́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pronicátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проницательный.html>проница́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pronicátelʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)проница́тельнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)проница́тельней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>perspicacious, acute, shrewd, astute

***проносить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проносить.html>проноси́ть</a> (23978)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проносить.html>проноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pronosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронести.html>пронести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to carry <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something through something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Им <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрешать.html>разреша́ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проносить.html>проноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>собо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>еду́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:напиток.html>напи́тки</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Im ne razrešáli <b>pronosítʹ</b> s sobój jedú i napítki.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">They were not allowed <b>to carry</b> food and drinks with them.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause (bad) diarrhea
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проносить.html>проно́сит</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>pronósit</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has bad diarrhea</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проносить.html>проноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pronosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прона́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to carry, to have
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проносить.html>проноси́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бутылка.html>буты́лку</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná vesʹ denʹ <b>pronosíla</b> étu butýlku.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She <b>carried</b> this bottle all day.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wear out</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропадать.html>пропада́ть</a> (3143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пропад-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">propad-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропадать.html>пропада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>пропа́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get lost, to be done</li>
<li>to disappear, to vanish</li>
<li>to lose, to fail</li>
<li>to perish, to die</li>
<li>to be wasted</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропащий.html>пропа́щий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">propáščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропадать.html>пропа́дать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propádatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>

***пропасть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>пропасть</a> (4015)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>про́пасть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">própastʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>про́пасти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>про́пасти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>про́пастей</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>пропасте́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>precipice, abyss, chasm</li>
<li>lots, tons</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Proto-Slavic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропасть.html>пропа́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propástʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропадать.html>пропада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get lost, to be done</li>
<li>to disappear, to vanish</li>
<li>to lose, to fail</li>
<li>to perish, to die</li>
<li>to be wasted</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропащий.html>пропа́щий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">propaščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>па́сть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 7b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:пропадать.html>пропада́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пропас-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропахнуть.html>пропа́хнуть</a> (13333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пахнуть.html>па́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">páxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропахнуть.html>пропа́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propáxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пропа́хивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smell of, to become permeated with the smell of <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пропахший.html>пропа́хший</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нафталин.html>нафтали́ном</a> (устаре́лый)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>propáxšij</b> naftalínom (ustarélyj)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">moth-eaten; antediluvian</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start to stink due to having spoiled
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́ба</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пропахнуть.html>пропа́хла</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rýba <b>propáxla</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the fish has started to smell</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пахнуть.html>па́х</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нуть</b>
